## 2026-07-23 — Articulation + physics round (build-117 device feedback)

**Decision:** joints may only bend as a reasonably flexible athletic human's do, and the mass model must satisfy real mechanics — both enforced by law, not per-move care. New invariants: `hangingHandsFoldOverTheBar` (a hanging hand bears load inside the wrap's palm-to-finger arc, thumb inward — the build-117 backwards wrap is unrepresentable), `hingesKeepTheirAxis` (swing-twist decomposition: elbows/knees/toes cannot bend off their hinge plane beyond the fleet's device-validated envelope; elbow roll = varus/valgus capped ±3°), `standingMovesBalanceTheirMomentum` (the zero-moment point — CoM projection shifted by the cart-table acceleration term, dt 0.25 s spanning bake knots, pad 0.075 for the conservative sole-corner polygon and un-authored preparatory sway — stays inside the contact-derived support polygon; ballistic moves belong to the ballistic law end-to-end), `nothingOutrunsGravity` (no grounded CoM accelerates down faster than free fall), `hangingMovesHangUnderTheBar` (pendulum equilibrium: strict ≤5 cm at still phases, ≤10 cm mid-rep — a gripped bar carries real torque), plus synthetic sway/2-g-drop provers on the ballistic-harness pattern. Wrist deviation tightened to a human ±40° (table + both arm solvers at ±38; squat 42→39, goblet 43→39 with the cup re-pocketed at wrist (46, 20, 39), 2.0 mm). **Kettlebell swing re-authored:** reps start/end STANDING with the bell hanging (analytic wrist (13.7, 24.0, 12.1), 0.0° off the handle), the float is a one-beat weightless turnaround with a hip-extension counterlean, gravity owns both descents, and the rest beat breathes at the stand — the old cycle held and rested at the float, a levitation. **Pull-Up is OUT of the catalog pending re-author:** its new hang/top configs pass every law (scratch-descent winners, one Euler sheet), but the path between them needs a better-conditioned station pin — the roll-bisection whips between solutions mid-pull (17 mm palm drift, spline teleports). Lessons banked: Euler-sheet path compatibility (legal endpoints in different sheets lerp through garbage), legs-solve-the-pendulum (grip solved by the arm, CoM by hips/knees — orthogonal), ZMP estimators must span bake knots, and a law's calibration needs a synthetic prover the moment tolerance grows.

**Reason:** Dave's build-117 device pass: pull-up fingers bent backwards around the bar with crossed elbows ("the mascot must only be able to bend its joints the way a reasonably flexible and athletic person would — figure out how to enforce that"), plus "fix the kettlebell swing and physics" with the per-part mass/CoM + momentum-laws prescription.

## 2026-07-23 — Today-view design review round 2b: headings off the rail, "=" retired everywhere, workouts not sessions, and the schedule anchor (Dave-decided item by item)

**Decision:** Dave decided all eight findings from the Today-view review (screenshot + code audit, review artifact): (1) the CARRIED OVER explainer caption is DELETED, not fixed — it truncated mid-sentence on device ("do them whe…"); (2) the week tally says **workouts**, never "sessions" (#144: performed things are workouts; the type name had leaked), both sites — Today header + finish recap; (3) **the rail's all-caps headings die** (TODAY · CARRIED OVER · BEYOND THIS WEEK): the timeline's state grammar (dashed grey "not yet" / solid green + Start "now" / amber + "was wed" "carried" / purple seal "done") carries the structure alone. The date line ("thu · jul 23") STAYS — it's today's label, the tense system's pivot, and the opening scroll's landing; the cadence lines stay as the unlabeled far end. This also dissolves the review's IA finding — BEYOND THIS WEEK read as a section header for the next-7-days cards below it, which are not beyond this week; (4) **"=" renders NOWHERE** — not the pending card's all-unchanged collapse, not "n =" tails, not the recap tally's per-line "=", not the live set card's "last 130 · =" (supersedes the #246-era keep-it-legible call: `RoutineDiff.summary` no longer emits unchanged segments and `Segment.Kind.unchanged` is deleted; the recap tally lists only movers and hides entirely when nothing moved; a zero live delta shows just "last 130"); (5) the committed card's net-gain chip and the start tray's "today" pill move from stroked capsules to the soft r6 `CardTagCapsule` (accent-tinted) — the two data tags the 2026-07-20 shape sweep missed; (6) `BlockBar` a11y: bars beside captions are hidden from VoiceOver (the caption states the fact; the bar announced a bare "2 of 4"), the captionless live set bar gains a "Sets" label; (7) rail fact captions (dates, estimates, cadences, the pending meta + diff line) reflow to 2 lines at accessibility sizes (`factLineLimit`) — #164's reflow-don't-cap extended from headings to the rail; names stay 1-line; (8) the future card's vertical padding aligns with the missed card at 10 pt (same anatomy, same rhythm).

**Same PR — the Friday-upcoming bug (Dave's device report): a schedule never carries or banks a day it wasn't around for.** Scheduling a routine for Friday on Thursday hid tomorrow's occurrence: the reconstruction read a completion from earlier that week as a "genuine extra" (nothing outstanding on its day) and banked Friday — because the schedule has no memory of when it was set, #354's `createdAt` anchor covered only ADDING the routine. Fix, two halves: (a) Kit `occurrenceSatisfiedEarly` gains the guard that a completion **on or before the anchor day never banks** a future occurrence (it predates the plan it would be "extra" to; on-the-anchor-day included, since day granularity can't order a same-day workout vs schedule edit — the safe error is showing the occurrence); (b) the app grows `Routine.scheduleChangedAt` (optional additive column, lightweight migration, nil = anchor at `createdAt`; stamped in the `schedule` SETTER on real value changes only, so every write path — tray, Operator, undo, interchange import — funnels through one stamp and a sync pull writing the same value back can't move the anchor; EXCLUDED from the interchange like `uuid`) and passes `scheduleAnchor = max(createdAt, scheduleChangedAt)` as the Kit's `addedOn` everywhere (TodayView due/upcoming, finish-screen next-up, widget snapshot). Side effect, intended: re-scheduling mon→fri also stops phantom past-Friday carries the new schedule never owned. Known trade, documented: banking by a genuine extra done the SAME day the schedule was configured is lost (day granularity); a repo restore stamps schedules fresh, suppressing pre-restore carried days once. Kit 462 green on Linux (+3 regression tests: pre-anchor completions never bank, same-day never banks, post-anchor banking unchanged).

**Reason:** Dave's notes on the review artifact, one call per finding, plus his device repro of the Friday miss. The heading drop is the biggest visual change: the rail's redundant channels (border, node color, caption tense) had made the labels decoration — and one of them was mislabeling its section while another truncated. ⚠️ Device pass: the unlabeled rail's readability on a real timeline (especially carried cards with no section intro), the r6 accent tags beside r11 keys, caption reflow at accessibility sizes, and the Thursday-schedule-Friday-shows repro on Dave's store.
